The temporary booking of other houses is not the price set in advance. Finally, I had to add a bed.

This should be the longest review I have given to the hotel. It is really a happy family experience. I stayed here two years ago and liked it very much and recommended it to many friends. This time it was really a pity...
The first thing worth praising is that the heated swimming pool in the single-family villa is also good (the swimming pools in the townhouses cannot be used); second, the attitude of the hotel front desk and the service staff who come to the room are very good; third, the hotel breakfast is good. .
However, it is said that the hardware is old and the service is impeccable. The current management team of this hotel is still very good, especially the service attitude is very correct. Although it is a third-party package, the hotel still called two days in advance to inquire about the details of check-in requirements, and then There are also housekeepers who add WeChat to provide 24-hour service. And it is also very kind in terms of room type upgrades. Platinum card members have been upgraded to a 220-square-meter detached pool villa, which is much more private than the booked townhouse pool villa.
.
The villa is arranged in the one closest to the lobby. It was very convenient to have breakfast in the past. There is a gap between the swimming pool and the road below, and the vegetation is lush, and the privacy is also very good. When entering the room, I found that the swimming pool has been placed for communication. Said the unicorn I wanted, and put two more, this is also the most beautiful unicorn I have ever seen, and it also has two-color wings! Give the butler a thumbs up! There are more than ten kinds of beverages and snacks in the minibar, which are replenished free of charge every day, and customized according to my requirements. This is the service level that a luxury hotel should have.
.
The 220 square meters should include the yard and swimming pool area. In fact, the interior space is the same as the townhouse garden view villa and townhouse pool villa. It is equivalent to a double bed room without a living room. To be honest, although there is an independent cloakroom, the interior space is still quite cramped, but according to the fact that this single-family villa in Haitang Bay only sells for 2,000 a night, it is still very cost-effective.
.
The entrance to the villa has a walkway leading directly to the swimming pool. The gate and the room door share the same room card. When you enter the door, you will find the minibar and cloakroom. The bedroom is on the left and the bathroom is on the right. The bedding and mattresses in the bedroom are quite comfortable, and the pillows are well supported. Soft, there is a desk against the wall, and a large fruit plate is given every day.
.
The bedroom door leads to the swimming pool, which is separated by a deck chair and a coffee table. In fact, this setting is a bit of a hindrance. I prefer the kind of swimming pool that can be jumped into by pushing the door, such as Pullman and Banyan Tree. The water in the swimming pool is constantly circulating, and it is very clean. Fallen leaves and other sundries are much better than Banyan Tree.
.
The bathroom has double basins on both sides, and the bathtub is placed in the middle. The body feels very comfortable. There are Herm√®s and Ruihua standard accessories, bath salt loofah, etc. for spare parts. There is no smart toilet, and the shower control is a bit old. The bathroom facilities have not kept up with the times. It is also not in line with Ruihua's positioning, and these are in urgent need of updating.
.
Other than that, everything is good, the room service responds very quickly, and being woken up by the melodious birdsong every day is also a pleasant experience.
